(*******************************************************************

 Lifting pseudofunctors to monads

 If we have a pseudofunctor from `B₁` to `B₂`, then we can lift it
 to a pseudofunctor from `mnd B₁` to `mnd B₂`.

 Contents
 1. Action on monads
 2. Action on monad morphisms
 3. Action on monad cells
 4. The identitor
 5. The compositor
 6. The pseudofunctor

 *******************************************************************)
Require Import UniMath.Foundations.All.

(**
 1. Action on monads
 *)
Section PsfunctorOnMonad.
  Context {B₁ B₂ : bicat}
          (F : psfunctor B₁ B₂)
          (m : mnd B₁).

  Let Fm : B₂ := F (ob_of_mnd m).
  Let Fe : Fm --> Fm := #F (endo_of_mnd m).
  Let Fη : id₁ Fm ==> Fe := psfunctor_id F _ • ##F (unit_of_mnd m).
  Let Fμ : Fe · Fe ==> Fe := psfunctor_comp F _ _ • ##F (mult_of_mnd m).

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
Fm:= F (ob_of_mnd m): B₂
Fe:= # F (endo_of_mnd m): B₂ ⟦ Fm, Fm ⟧
Fη:= psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
• ## F (unit_of_mnd m): id₁ Fm ==> Fe
Fμ:= psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
• ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe · Fe ==> Fe
(linvunitor Fe • (Fη ▹ Fe)) • Fμ = id₂ Fe

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
Fm:= F (ob_of_mnd m): B₂
Fe:= # F (endo_of_mnd m): B₂ ⟦ Fm, Fm ⟧
Fη:= psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
• ## F (unit_of_mnd m): id₁ Fm ==> Fe
Fμ:= psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
• ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe · Fe ==> Fe
(linvunitor Fe • (Fη ▹ Fe)) • Fμ = id₂ Fe

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
Fm:= F (ob_of_mnd m): B₂
Fe:= # F (endo_of_mnd m): B₂ ⟦ Fm, Fm ⟧
Fη:= psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
• ## F (unit_of_mnd m): id₁ Fm ==> Fe
Fμ:= psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
• ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe · Fe ==> Fe
(linvunitor (# F (endo_of_mnd m))
 • ((psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
     • ## F (unit_of_mnd m)) ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m)))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
   • ## F (mult_of_mnd m)) = id₂ (# F (endo_of_mnd m))

• ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe · Fe ==> Fe
(linvunitor (# F (endo_of_mnd m))
 • ((psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
     • ## F (unit_of_mnd m)) ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m)))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
   • ## F (mult_of_mnd m)) =
## F (id₂ (endo_of_mnd m))

    • (unit_of_mnd m ▹ endo_of_mnd m)) • mult_of_mnd m)

B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
Fm:= F (ob_of_mnd m): B₂
Fe:= # F (endo_of_mnd m): B₂ ⟦ Fm, Fm ⟧
Fη:= psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
• ## F (unit_of_mnd m): id₁ Fm ==> Fe
Fμ:= psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
• ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe · Fe ==> Fe
(linvunitor (# F (endo_of_mnd m))
 • ((psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
     • ## F (unit_of_mnd m)) ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m)))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
   • ## F (mult_of_mnd m)) =
(((linvunitor (# F (endo_of_mnd m))
   • (psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)

 • ## F (unit_of_mnd m ▹ endo_of_mnd m))
• ## F (mult_of_mnd m)

 • ((psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
     ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m))
    • (## F (unit_of_mnd m) ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m))))

      ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m)))
  • psfunctor_comp F (id₁ (ob_of_mnd m))
      (endo_of_mnd m))
 • ## F (unit_of_mnd m ▹ endo_of_mnd m))
• ## F (mult_of_mnd m)

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
Fm:= F (ob_of_mnd m): B₂
Fe:= # F (endo_of_mnd m): B₂ ⟦ Fm, Fm ⟧
Fη:= psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
• ## F (unit_of_mnd m): id₁ Fm ==> Fe

• ((psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m) ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m))
   • ((## F (unit_of_mnd m) ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m))
      • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m)
           (endo_of_mnd m) • ## F (mult_of_mnd m)))) =
linvunitor (# F (endo_of_mnd m))
• ((psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m) ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m))
   • (psfunctor_comp F (id₁ (ob_of_mnd m))
        (endo_of_mnd m)
      • (## F (unit_of_mnd m ▹ endo_of_mnd m)
         • ## F (mult_of_mnd m))))

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
Fm:= F (ob_of_mnd m): B₂
Fe:= # F (endo_of_mnd m): B₂ ⟦ Fm, Fm ⟧
Fη:= psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
• ## F (unit_of_mnd m): id₁ Fm ==> Fe
Fμ:= psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
• ## F (mult_of_mnd m): Fe · Fe ==> Fe
(## F (unit_of_mnd m) ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)
   • ## F (mult_of_mnd m)) =
psfunctor_comp F (id₁ (ob_of_mnd m)) (endo_of_mnd m)
• (## F (unit_of_mnd m ▹ endo_of_mnd m)
   • ## F (mult_of_mnd m))

m: mnd B₁

 • ## F (unit_of_mnd m ▹ endo_of_mnd m))
• ## F (mult_of_mnd m)

• psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m) (endo_of_mnd m)

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

(rinvunitor Fe • (Fe ◃ Fη)) • Fμ = id₂ Fe

   • ## F (mult_of_mnd m))

    ◃ pr122 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe Fη Fμ)))

(rassociator (pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe Fη Fμ))
   (pr2
      (pr1 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe Fη Fμ),,
       pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe Fη Fμ)))
   (pr2
      (pr1 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe Fη Fμ),,
       pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe Fη Fμ)))

    ◃ pr222 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe Fη Fμ)))

 ▹ pr12 (make_mnd_data Fm Fe Fη Fμ))

(**
 2. Action on monad morphisms
 *)
Section PsfunctorOnMonadMor.
  Context {B₁ B₂ : bicat}
          (F : psfunctor B₁ B₂)
          {m₁ m₂ : mnd B₁}
          (f : m₁ --> m₂).

  Let Ff : F (ob_of_mnd m₁) --> F (ob_of_mnd m₂)
    := #F (mor_of_mnd_mor f).
  Let Fe : Ff · # F (endo_of_mnd m₂) ==> # F (endo_of_mnd m₁) · Ff
      := psfunctor_comp F _ _
         • ##F (mnd_mor_endo f)
         • (psfunctor_comp F _ _)^-1.

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B₂ ⟦ F (ob_of_mnd m₁), F (ob_of_mnd m₂) ⟧
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff · # F (endo_of_mnd m₂) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m₁) · Ff
linvunitor Ff
• (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁) ▹ Ff) =
(rinvunitor Ff
 • (Ff ◃ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂))) • Fe

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B₂ ⟦ F (ob_of_mnd m₁), F (ob_of_mnd m₂) ⟧
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff · # F (endo_of_mnd m₂) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m₁) · Ff
linvunitor Ff
• (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁) ▹ Ff) =
(rinvunitor Ff
 • (Ff ◃ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂))) • Fe

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧

   ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =

 • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ◃ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂)))

      (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
   • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B₂ ⟦ F (ob_of_mnd m₁), F (ob_of_mnd m₂) ⟧
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff · # F (endo_of_mnd m₂) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m₁) · Ff
p:= maponpaths
  (λ z : mor_of_mnd_mor f ==>
         endo_of_mnd m₁ · mor_of_mnd_mor f, ## F z)
  (mnd_mor_unit f): (λ z : mor_of_mnd_mor f ==>
       endo_of_mnd m₁ · mor_of_mnd_mor f, ## F z)
  (linvunitor (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   • (unit_of_mnd m₁ ▹ mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(λ z : mor_of_mnd_mor f ==>
       endo_of_mnd m₁ · mor_of_mnd_mor f, ## F z)
  ((rinvunitor (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    • (mor_of_mnd_mor f ◃ unit_of_mnd m₂))
   • mnd_mor_endo f)
linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
• (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁)
   ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ◃ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂)))

   • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)

      • psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
          (mor_of_mnd_mor f))) =
rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
• ((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ◃ psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m₂))
   • (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
        (id₁ (ob_of_mnd m₂))
      • (## F (mor_of_mnd_mor f ◃ unit_of_mnd m₂)
         • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))))
((psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m₁)
  • ## F (unit_of_mnd m₁)) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
• psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁) (mor_of_mnd_mor f) =
((psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m₁)
  ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 • (## F (unit_of_mnd m₁) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)))
• psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁) (mor_of_mnd_mor f)

      
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B₂ ⟦ F (ob_of_mnd m₁), F (ob_of_mnd m₂) ⟧
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff · # F (endo_of_mnd m₂) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m₁) · Ff
p: linvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
• ((psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m₁)
    ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
   • ((## F (unit_of_mnd m₁)
       ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
      • psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
          (mor_of_mnd_mor f))) =
rinvunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
• ((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    ◃ psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m₂))
   • (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
        (id₁ (ob_of_mnd m₂))
      • (## F (mor_of_mnd_mor f ◃ unit_of_mnd m₂)
         • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))))
(psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m₁) • ## F (unit_of_mnd m₁))
▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f) =
(psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m₁)
 ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
• (## F (unit_of_mnd m₁) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))

(psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m₁) • ## F (unit_of_mnd m₁))

B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B₂ ⟦ F (ob_of_mnd m₁), F (ob_of_mnd m₂) ⟧
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff · # F (endo_of_mnd m₂) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m₁) · Ff
((((lassociator Ff (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂))
      (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂))
    • (Fe ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m₂)))
   • rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁)) Ff
       (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂)))
  • (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁) ◃ Fe))
 • lassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁))
     (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁)) Ff)
• (mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁) ▹ Ff) =
(Ff ◃ mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂)) • Fe

B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂

Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B₂ ⟦ F (ob_of_mnd m₁), F (ob_of_mnd m₂) ⟧
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))

     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff · # F (endo_of_mnd m₂) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m₁) · Ff
((((lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
      (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂)) (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂))
    • (((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
           (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
        • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
             (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)
       ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m₂)))
   • rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁))
       (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂)))
  • (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
     ◃ ((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
           (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
        • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
             (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)))

     (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)))

   ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =

        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)

       (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂)))
  • (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁)
     ◃ pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)))
 • lassociator (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁))
     (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁))
     (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)))
• (mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁)
   ▹ pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)) =
(pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
 ◃ mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂))
• pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)

      
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B₂ ⟦ F (ob_of_mnd m₁), F (ob_of_mnd m₂) ⟧
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff · # F (endo_of_mnd m₂) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m₁) · Ff
linvunitor (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
• (unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁)
   ▹ pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)) =
(rinvunitor (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
 • (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
    ◃ unit_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂)))
• pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
 exact psfunctor_on_mnd_mor_unit.
      
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
Ff:= # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f): B₂ ⟦ F (ob_of_mnd m₁), F (ob_of_mnd m₂) ⟧
Fe:= (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1: Ff · # F (endo_of_mnd m₂) ==>
# F (endo_of_mnd m₁) · Ff
((((lassociator (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
      (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂))
      (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂))
    • (pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
       ▹ endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂)))
   • rassociator (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁))
       (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe))
       (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂)))
  • (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁)
     ◃ pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)))
 • lassociator (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁))
     (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁))
     (pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)))
• (mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁)
   ▹ pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)) =
(pr1 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
 ◃ mult_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₂))
• pr2 (make_mnd_mor_data Ff Fe)
 exact psfunctor_on_mnd_mor_mu.
  Defined.
End PsfunctorOnMonadMor.

(**
 3. Action on monad cells
 *)

B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f, g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
τ: f ==> g
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ==> psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g


B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f, g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
τ: f ==> g
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f ==> psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f, g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
τ: f ==> g
mnd_cell_data (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f)
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f, g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
τ: f ==> g
is_mnd_cell ?τ

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f, g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
τ: f ==> g
mnd_cell_data (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f)
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
 exact (##F (cell_of_mnd_cell τ)).
  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂: mnd B₁
f, g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
τ: f ==> g
is_mnd_cell (## F (cell_of_mnd_cell τ))
 abstract
      (unfold is_mnd_cell ;
       cbn -[psfunctor_comp psfunctor_id] ;
       rewrite !vassocr ;
       rewrite <- psfunctor_rwhisker ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       apply maponpaths ;
       rewrite !vassocr ;
       rewrite <- psfunctor_vcomp ;
       rewrite <- (mnd_cell_endo τ) ;
       rewrite !psfunctor_vcomp ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       apply maponpaths ;
       use vcomp_move_R_pM ; [ is_iso | ] ;
       rewrite !vassocr ;
       use vcomp_move_L_Mp ; [ is_iso | ] ;
       cbn -[psfunctor_comp psfunctor_id] ;
       rewrite psfunctor_lwhisker ;
       apply idpath).
Defined.

(**
 4. The identitor
 *)

B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
id₁ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m) ==>
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id₁ m)


B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
id₁ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m) ==>
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id₁ m)

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
mnd_cell_data (id₁ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m))
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id₁ m))
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
is_mnd_cell ?τ

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
mnd_cell_data (id₁ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m))
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id₁ m))
 
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
mor_of_mnd_mor (id₁ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m)) ==>
mor_of_mnd_mor (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id₁ m))

    exact (psfunctor_id F _).
  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m: mnd B₁
is_mnd_cell
  (psfunctor_id F (ob_of_mnd m)
   :
   mnd_cell_data (id₁ (psfunctor_on_mnd F m))
     (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (id₁ m)))
 abstract
      (unfold is_mnd_cell ;
       cbn -[psfunctor_id psfunctor_comp] ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       rewrite !psfunctor_vcomp ;
       rewrite psfunctor_lunitor ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       do 3 apply maponpaths ;
       rewrite psfunctor_rinvunitor ;
       rewrite !vassocl ;
       rewrite vcomp_rinv ;
       rewrite id2_right ;
       apply idpath).
Defined.

(**
 5. The compositor
 *)
Section PsfunctorOnMonadComposition.
  Context {B₁ B₂ : bicat}
          (F : psfunctor B₁ B₂)
          {m₁ m₂ m₃ : mnd B₁}
          (f : m₁ --> m₂)
          (g : m₂ --> m₃).

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
mnd_mor_endo
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f · psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
• (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁)
   ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
 ▹ endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₃))
• mnd_mor_endo (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f · g))

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
mnd_mor_endo
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f · psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
• (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁)
   ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
 ▹ endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₃))
• mnd_mor_endo (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f · g))

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
((((rassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
      (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) (# F (endo_of_mnd m₃))
    • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       ◃ ((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
             (endo_of_mnd m₃) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo g))
          • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₂)
               (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) ^-1)))
   • lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
       (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
  • (((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
      • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
           (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)
     ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
 • rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁))
     (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
• (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
   ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
 ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m₃))
• ((psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f · pr1 g) (endo_of_mnd m₃)
    • ## F
        ((((rassociator (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr112 m₃)
            • (pr1 f ◃ pr112 g))
           • lassociator (pr1 f) (pr112 m₂) (pr1 g))
          • (pr112 f ▹ pr1 g))
         • rassociator (pr112 m₁) (pr1 f) (pr1 g)))
   • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
        (pr1 f · pr1 g)) ^-1)

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
((((rassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
      (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) (# F (endo_of_mnd m₃))
    • (((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
             (endo_of_mnd m₃))
        • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
           ◃ ## F (mnd_mor_endo g)))
       • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
          ◃ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₂)
               (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) ^-1)))
   • lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
       (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
  • (((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         (endo_of_mnd m₂) • ## F (mnd_mor_endo f))
      • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
           (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1)
     ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
 • rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁))
     (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
• (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
   ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
 ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m₃))
• ((psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f · pr1 g) (endo_of_mnd m₃)
    • ## F
        ((((rassociator (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr112 m₃)
            • (pr1 f ◃ pr112 g))
           • lassociator (pr1 f) (pr112 m₂) (pr1 g))
          • (pr112 f ▹ pr1 g))
         • rassociator (pr112 m₁) (pr1 f) (pr1 g)))
   • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
        (pr1 f · pr1 g)) ^-1)

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
((((rassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
      (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) (# F (endo_of_mnd m₃))
    • (((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
             (endo_of_mnd m₃))
        • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
           ◃ ## F (mnd_mor_endo g)))
       • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
          ◃ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₂)
               (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) ^-1)))
   • lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
       (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
  • (((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         (endo_of_mnd m₂) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g))
      • (## F (mnd_mor_endo f)
         ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
     • ((psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
           (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1
        ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g))))
 • rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁))
     (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
• (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
   ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
 ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m₃))
• ((psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f · pr1 g) (endo_of_mnd m₃)
    • ## F
        ((((rassociator (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr112 m₃)
            • (pr1 f ◃ pr112 g))
           • lassociator (pr1 f) (pr112 m₂) (pr1 g))
          • (pr112 f ▹ pr1 g))
         • rassociator (pr112 m₁) (pr1 f) (pr1 g)))
   • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
        (pr1 f · pr1 g)) ^-1)

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
((((rassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
      (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) (# F (endo_of_mnd m₃))
    • (((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
             (endo_of_mnd m₃))
        • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
           ◃ ## F (mnd_mor_endo g)))
       • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
          ◃ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₂)
               (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) ^-1)))
   • lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
       (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
  • (((psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         (endo_of_mnd m₂) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g))
      • (## F (mnd_mor_endo f)
         ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
     • ((psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
           (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1
        ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g))))
 • rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁))
     (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
• (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
   ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
 ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m₃))
• ((psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f · pr1 g) (endo_of_mnd m₃)
    • ((((## F
            (rassociator (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr112 m₃))
          • ## F (pr1 f ◃ pr112 g))
         • ## F
             (lassociator (pr1 f) (pr112 m₂) (pr1 g)))
        • ## F (pr112 f ▹ pr1 g))
       • ## F (rassociator (pr112 m₁) (pr1 f) (pr1 g))))
   • (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
        (pr1 f · pr1 g)) ^-1)

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
((((((((rassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
          (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g))
          (# F (endo_of_mnd m₃))
        • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
           ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
               (endo_of_mnd m₃)))
       • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
          ◃ ## F (mnd_mor_endo g)))
      • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         ◃ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₂)
              (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) ^-1))
     • lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
         (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂))
         (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
    • (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         (endo_of_mnd m₂) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
   • (## F (mnd_mor_endo f) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
  • ((psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1
     ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
 • rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁))
     (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
• (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
   ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(((((((psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g)
       ▹ # F (endo_of_mnd m₃))
      • psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f · pr1 g)
          (endo_of_mnd m₃))
     • ## F (rassociator (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr112 m₃)))
    • ## F (pr1 f ◃ pr112 g))
   • ## F (lassociator (pr1 f) (pr112 m₂) (pr1 g)))
  • ## F (pr112 f ▹ pr1 g))
 • ## F (rassociator (pr112 m₁) (pr1 f) (pr1 g)))
• (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁) (pr1 f · pr1 g))
  ^-1

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
((((((((rassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
          (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g))
          (# F (endo_of_mnd m₃))
        • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
           ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
               (endo_of_mnd m₃)))
       • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
          ◃ ## F (mnd_mor_endo g)))
      • (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         ◃ (psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₂)
              (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) ^-1))
     • lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
         (# F (endo_of_mnd m₂))
         (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
    • (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
         (endo_of_mnd m₂) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
   • (## F (mnd_mor_endo f) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
  • ((psfunctor_comp F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
        (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) ^-1
     ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
 • rassociator (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁))
     (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)))
• (# F (endo_of_mnd m₁)
   ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
((((((rassociator (# F (pr1 f)) (# F (pr1 g))
        (# F (pr112 m₃))
      • (# F (pr1 f)
         ◃ psfunctor_comp F (pr1 g) (pr112 m₃)))
     • psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr1 g · pr112 m₃))
    • ## F (pr1 f ◃ pr112 g))
   • ## F (lassociator (pr1 f) (pr112 m₂) (pr1 g)))
  • ## F (pr112 f ▹ pr1 g))
 • ## F (rassociator (pr112 m₁) (pr1 f) (pr1 g)))

• (## F (pr1 f ◃ pr112 g)
   • (## F (lassociator (pr1 f) (pr112 m₂) (pr1 g))
      • ## F (pr112 f ▹ pr1 g)))

B₁, B₂: bicat

B₁, B₂: bicat

    (endo_of_mnd m₂ · pr1 g) =
(# F (pr1 f) ◃ ## F (pr112 g))
• psfunctor_comp F (pr1 f) (pr112 m₂ · pr1 g)

    apply idpath.
  Qed.

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f · psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g ==>
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f · g)

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f · psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g ==>
psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f · g)

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
mnd_cell_data
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f · psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f · g))
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
is_mnd_cell ?τ

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
mnd_cell_data
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f · psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f · g))
 
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
mor_of_mnd_mor
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f · psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g) ==>
mor_of_mnd_mor (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f · g))

      exact (psfunctor_comp F _ _).
    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
is_mnd_cell
  (psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
     (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
   :
   mnd_cell_data
     (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f
      · psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
     (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f · g)))
 
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
m₁, m₂, m₃: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₁, m₂ ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ m₂, m₃ ⟧
mnd_mor_endo
  (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f · psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F g)
• (endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₁)
   ◃ psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
       (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) =
(psfunctor_comp F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
   (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
 ▹ endo_of_mnd (psfunctor_on_mnd F m₃))
• mnd_mor_endo (psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F (f · g))

      exact psfunctor_on_mnd_comp_mor_endo.
  Defined.
End PsfunctorOnMonadComposition.

(*
 6. The pseudofunctor
 *)
Section LiftPsfunctorToMonad.
  Context {B₁ B₂ : bicat}
          (F : psfunctor B₁ B₂).

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
psfunctor_data (mnd B₁) (mnd B₂)

  
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
psfunctor_data (mnd B₁) (mnd B₂)

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
mnd B₁ → mnd B₂
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
∏ a b : mnd B₁,
mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧ → mnd B₂ ⟦ ?F₀ a, ?F₀ b ⟧
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
∏ (a b : mnd B₁) (f g : mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧),
f ==> g → ?F₁ a b f ==> ?F₁ a b g
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
∏ a : mnd B₁, id₁ (?F₀ a) ==> ?F₁ a a (id₁ a)
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
∏ (a b c : mnd B₁) (f : mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧)
(g : mnd B₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧),
?F₁ a b f · ?F₁ b c g ==> ?F₁ a c (f · g)

    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
mnd B₁ → mnd B₂
 exact (psfunctor_on_mnd F).
    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
∏ a b : mnd B₁,
mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
→ mnd B₂ ⟦ psfunctor_on_mnd F a, psfunctor_on_mnd F b
  ⟧
 exact (λ _ _ f, psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f).
    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
∏ (a b : mnd B₁) (f g : mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧),
f ==> g
→ (λ (a0 b0 : mnd B₁) (f0 : mnd B₁ ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧),
   psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f0) a b f ==>
  (λ (a0 b0 : mnd B₁) (f0 : mnd B₁ ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧),
   psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f0) a b g
 exact (λ _ _ _ _ τ, psfunctor_on_mnd_cell F τ).
    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
∏ a : mnd B₁,
id₁ (psfunctor_on_mnd F a) ==>
(λ (a0 b : mnd B₁) (f : mnd B₁ ⟦ a0, b ⟧),
 psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f) a a (id₁ a)
 exact (psfunctor_on_mnd_id_mor F).
    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
∏ (a b c : mnd B₁) (f : mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧)
(g : mnd B₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧),
(λ (a0 b0 : mnd B₁) (f0 : mnd B₁ ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧),
 psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f0) a b f
· (λ (a0 b0 : mnd B₁) (f0 : mnd B₁ ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧),
   psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f0) b c g ==>
(λ (a0 b0 : mnd B₁) (f0 : mnd B₁ ⟦ a0, b0 ⟧),
 psfunctor_on_mnd_mor F f0) a c (f · g)
 exact (λ _ _ _ f g, psfunctor_on_mnd_comp_mor F f g).
  Defined.

B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
a, b: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
## F (id₂ (pr1 f)) = id₂ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
a, b: mnd B₁
f, g, h: mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
η: f ==> g
φ: g ==> h
## F (pr1 η • pr1 φ) =
## F (cell_of_mnd_cell η) • ## F (cell_of_mnd_cell φ)
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
a, b: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
lunitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
(((pr122 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a)
  ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 • (pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd a)
     (ob_of_mnd b) (id₁ (pr1 a)) (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
• ## F (lunitor (pr1 f))
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
a, b: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
runitor (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)) =
((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
  ◃ (pr122 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd b))
 • (pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd b)
     (ob_of_mnd b) (mor_of_mnd_mor f) (id₁ (pr1 b)))
• ## F (runitor (pr1 f))
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
a, b, c, d: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧
h: mnd B₁ ⟦ c, d ⟧
((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
  ◃ (pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd b) (ob_of_mnd c)
      (ob_of_mnd d) (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
      (mor_of_mnd_mor h))
 • (pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd b)
     (ob_of_mnd d) (mor_of_mnd_mor f) (pr1 g · pr1 h))
• ## F (lassociator (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr1 h)) =
(lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
   (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor h))
 • ((pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd b)
      (ob_of_mnd c) (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
      (mor_of_mnd_mor g) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor h)))
• (pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd c)
    (ob_of_mnd d) (pr1 f · pr1 g) (mor_of_mnd_mor h)
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
a, b, c: mnd B₁
f: mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
g₁, g₂: mnd B₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧
η: g₁ ==> g₂
(pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd b)
  (ob_of_mnd c) (mor_of_mnd_mor f) (mor_of_mnd_mor g₁)
• ## F (pr1 f ◃ pr1 η) =
(# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f) ◃ ## F (cell_of_mnd_cell η))
• (pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd b)
    (ob_of_mnd c) (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    (mor_of_mnd_mor g₂)
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
a, b, c: mnd B₁
f₁, f₂: mnd B₁ ⟦ a, b ⟧
g: mnd B₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧
η: f₁ ==> f₂
(pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd b)
  (ob_of_mnd c) (mor_of_mnd_mor f₁) (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
• ## F (pr1 η ▹ pr1 g) =
(## F (cell_of_mnd_cell η) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g))
• (pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd b)
    (ob_of_mnd c) (mor_of_mnd_mor f₂)
    (mor_of_mnd_mor g)

## F (id₂ (pr1 f)) = id₂ (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
 apply psfunctor_id2.
    
B₁, B₂: bicat

φ: g ==> h
## F (pr1 η • pr1 φ) =

 apply psfunctor_vcomp.

  ◃ (pr122 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd b))
 • (pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd b)
     (ob_of_mnd b) (mor_of_mnd_mor f) (id₁ (pr1 b)))
• ## F (runitor (pr1 f))
 apply psfunctor_runitor.
    
B₁, B₂: bicat
F: psfunctor B₁ B₂
a, b, c, d: mnd B₁

g: mnd B₁ ⟦ b, c ⟧
h: mnd B₁ ⟦ c, d ⟧
((# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
  ◃ (pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd b) (ob_of_mnd c)
      (ob_of_mnd d) (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
      (mor_of_mnd_mor h))
 • (pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd b)
     (ob_of_mnd d) (mor_of_mnd_mor f) (pr1 g · pr1 h))
• ## F (lassociator (pr1 f) (pr1 g) (pr1 h)) =
(lassociator (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f))
   (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor g)) (# F (mor_of_mnd_mor h))
 • ((pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd b)
      (ob_of_mnd c) (mor_of_mnd_mor f)

    (ob_of_mnd d) (pr1 f · pr1 g) (mor_of_mnd_mor h)
 apply psfunctor_lassociator.

(# F (mor_of_mnd_mor f) ◃ ## F (cell_of_mnd_cell η))

    (ob_of_mnd c) (mor_of_mnd_mor f)
    (mor_of_mnd_mor g₂)
 apply psfunctor_lwhisker.
    
B₁, B₂: bicat

(## F (cell_of_mnd_cell η) ▹ # F (mor_of_mnd_mor g))
• (pr222 (pr1 F)) (ob_of_mnd a) (ob_of_mnd b)
    (ob_of_mnd c) (mor_of_mnd_mor f₂)
    (mor_of_mnd_mor g)
 apply psfunctor_rwhisker.
  Qed.
